Typical Subway they have all the typical sandwich stuff. They also have a new wrap that's 6.99 but you get 2x the meat, which is the same portion as a footlong. They brought back a few $5 footlong sandwiches but the others are overpriced. The process typically compare to a deli or specialized sandwich place but the meat quality at Subway doesn't seem as great and the veggies don't always taste fresh. Personally it's good for a quick sandwich if you like the cheaper options but otherwise I'd prefer to spend $2 more and get a quality sandwich.< /review>

Their food is very messy. Almost as if they cared more about speed then presentation.  Their food isn't all that tasty either, aside from their enchiladas. Their tostada was disappointing and loaded with too much lettuce and onions and not enough shredded beef. Their burritos are also disappointing. Their prices are high for what the product is. All-in-all, if Im feeling Mexican food, I would hit up a taco truck before coming here.</Review>
